<p><a href="/dota2/Beyond_the_Summit" title="Beyond the Summit">Beyond the Summit</a> returns with season 3 of <b>BTS Pro Series</b>, an online event featuring tournaments for the Americas,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Europe/CIS,<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> and Southeast Asia.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=BTS/Pro_Series/3/Americas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Participants</b>
<ul><li>Nine invited teams</li>
<li>One team from the <a href="/dota2/BTS/Pro_Series/3/Americas/Open_Qualifier" title="BTS/Pro Series/3/Americas/Open Qualifier">open qualifier</a></li></ul></li>
<li><b>Group Stage</b>  -  <i>September 7th - 18th, 2020</i>
<ul><li>Single round-robin</li>
<li>All matches are <abbr title="Best-of-two">Bo2</abbr></li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(221,244,221);">Top four teams</span> advance to the upper bracket of the playoffs</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(249,240,199);">5th to 8th placed teams</span> advance to the lower bracket of the playoffs</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(251,223,223);">Bottom two teams</span> are eliminated</li>
<li><span class="mw-customtoggle-Tiebreaker" style="border-bottom:1px dotted;"><i>Click here for tiebreaker rules</i></span></li></ul></li></ul>
<div class="toccolours mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" id="mw-customcollapsible-Tiebreaker" style="width:760px; margin-left:45px">
<ol><li>Head-to-head match results between tied teams</li>
<li>Sonneborn-berger score (combined match score of the teams beaten)</li>
<li>Comparative match results against each team from the top down</li>
<li>Resets to the first metric if a partial tie is broken</li>
<li>In the case that the above process cannot break a tie that affects bracket placement or elimination, the Administration will decide when and how tiebreakers games will be played.</li></ol>
</div>
<ul><li><b>Playoffs</b>  -  <i>September 19th - 22nd, 2020</i>
<ul><li>Double-elimination bracket</li>
<li>Grand Final is <abbr title="Best-of-five">Bo5</abbr>, all other matches are <abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr></li></ul></li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Participants">Participants</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=BTS/Pro_Series/3/Americas&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Participants">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="max-width:120px"><div class="teamcard-toggle-button"></div></div>
<div style="max-width:1200px;"><div class="template-box" style="padding-right:2em;">
